 On the occasion of his birthday, we are sharing some important things related to him and his 10 thoughts with you
 1
 APJ Abdul Kalam was born on 15 October 1931 in Rameswaram in the South Indian state of Tamil Nadu
 2
 Kalam, a sailor by profession, was not well educated
 ye machuaaron ko naav kiraaye par diya karte the
 To run a family of five brothers and five sisters, the father's money was scarce, so to continue his early education, Kalam also had to sell newspapers
 4
 From the age of eight, Kalam used to get up at 4 in the morning and take a bath and go to study mathematics
 subah naha kar jane ke peeche kaaran yah tha ki prayek saal paanch bacchon ko muft main ganit padhaane vaale unke teacher bina nahaye aae bacchon ko nahin padhaate the
 After coming from tuition, he used to offer Namaz and after that he used to distribute news papers at Rameswaram railway station and bus stand till eight in the morning
 5
 Kalam tells Subrahmanyam Iyer, his fifth class teacher, to get into 'aerospace technology'
 wo kehete hai, ‘wo hamaare achche teachers main se the
 Once he asked in class how the bird flies? If no student of the class answered it, the next day they took all the children to the beach
 vahaan kai pakshi ud rahe the
 Some were coming down to the sea and some were sitting
 vahaan unhone hamen pakshi ke udne ke peeche ke kaaran ko samajhaayaa saath hi pakshiyon ke sharir kii banaavat ko bhi vistaar purvak bataaya jo udne main sahaayak hota he
 These things explained by him were so ingrained in me that i always felt that i am on the beach of Rameswaram and the incident that day inspired me to set the goal of life
 baad main maine tay kiya ki udaan kii disha main hi apana kariyar banaau
 i later studied physics and studied aeronautical engineering from Madras Engineering College
 ’6
 Kalam arrived in ISRO in 1962
 inhen ke project diarector rahete bharat ne apana pehla swadeshi upgrah prakshepan yaan eselvi-3 banaaya
 In 1980, the Rohini satellite was placed near the Earth's orbit and India became a member of the International Space Club
 kalam ne iske baad swadeshi gided missile ko dizin kiya
 They made missiles like Agni and Prithvi with Indian technology
 7
 From 1992 to 1999, Kalam was also the Defense Advisor to the Defense Minister
 is dauraan vaajapeyi sarkaar ne pokharan main duusari baar newclear test bhi kiye or bharat parmaanu hathiyaar banane vaale deshon main shaamil ho gaya
 Kalam gave Vision 2020
 iske tahat kalam ne bharat ko vigyaan ke kshetra main tarakkee ke jariye 2020 tak atyaadhunik karne kii khaas soch di gai
 Kalam was also the Chief Scientific Advisor to the Government of India
 8
 In 1982, Kalam was made the director of DRDL (defense Research Development Laboratory)
 usee dauraan anna uniwarsity ne unhen doctor kii oopaadhi se sammanit kiya
 Kalam then gave the Defense Minister's scientific advisor, Dr
 vies arunachalam ke saath integrated gided missile deveopment program (ijmdipi) kaa prastaav taiyaar kiya
 a committee was formed under the chairmanship of Kalam for the development of indigenous missiles
 iske pehle charan main jameen se jameen par madhyam duuri tak maar karne vaali missile banane par jor tha
 In the second phase, it was proposed to make ground-to-air missiles, antitank missiles and the Reintree Experiment Launch Vehicle (rex)
 prithvi, trishul, akaash, naag naam ke missile banaae gaye
 Kalam named his dream Rex as Agni
 sabase pehle sitambar 1985 main trishul phir farvari 1988 main prithvi or may 1989 main agni kaa pareekshan kiya gaya
 Subsequently, in 1998, India, along with Russia, started work on making supersonic cruise missiles and brahmos Private Limited was established
 brahmos ko dharti, aasmaan or samudr kahin bhi daagi ja sakati he
 With this success Kalam gained fame as a missile man and was awarded the Padma Vibhushan
 9
 Kalam was awarded the country's highest civilian honor, the Padma Bhushan in 1981, and then the Padma Vibhushan in 1990 and the Bharat Ratna in 1997
 bharat ke sarvocch par par niyukti se pehle bharat ratna paane vaale kalam desh ke keval tisare raashtrapati hai
 Sarvapalli Radhakrishnan and Zakir Hussain achieved this before them
 doctor apije abdul kalam ke kuch prasiddh kathan* sapane sach hon iske liye sapane dekhnaa jaruri he
 * The dreams of great dreamers are always excellent

 haalanki aapraadhik sajeesh kii dhara hathaaye jane ko lekar hycourt ne koi tippanee nahin kii thi
 The UP government did not correct the technical mistake and the FIR No
 198 case went back to Rae Bareli Court
 4 may 2001 main lakhanu kii sibiai court ke special jaj shrikant shukla ne adwani or 20 anya netaaon ke khilaaf aapraadhik sajeesh kii dhara hataa di kyonki exiaar 197 sirf babari masjid ke vidhwans ko lekar thi naa ki aapraadhik sajeesh ko lekar
 Later in May 2010, the Allahabad High Court also upheld this decision
 is faisle ke nau maheene ke baad ,farvari 2011 main sibiai ne supreme court main arji daayar kii
 Advani and the rest of the leaders were demanding that the petition be dismissed as the basis for the delay in filing the petition, but the court rejected the demand
 sibiai ke alaava ek yachikakarta haji mehboob ne bhi supreme court main arji lagaakar kaha tha ki 2014 main centre main sarkaar badalane ke baad sibiai apana rukh badal sakati he
 Accused of BJP and Sangh should be prosecuted under criminal conspiracy
 ab sibiai or haji mehboob kii yachika par sunwaayee puri ho gayi he or jald hi supreme court is maamle main apana faisla sunayega
 Kings XI Punjab defeated Delhi Daredevils by 10 wickets
 usne 68 ranon kaa maamuli lakshya 73 genden shesh rahete hasil kiya
 Hashim Amla and Martin Guptill 7
 5 over main bina kisi nuksaan ke 68 ran bana daale
 Guptill 50 and Amla returned unbeaten after scoring 16 runs
 sarvaadhik genden shesh rahete hue jeet hasil karne kaa record mumbai ke naam he
 He defeated KKR by 8 wickets in 2008 with 87 balls
 2011 main kochi taskars ne 76 gende shesh rahete rajasthan royles ko haraaya tha
 In this sense, this is Punjab's third major victory
 kings ilevan punjab ne ipel main pehali baar 10 wicket se jeet hasil kii he
 Punjab have kept their playop hopes alive with four wins from 9 matches
 jabaki dilli ko 8 maichon main chhathi haar mili he
 Sandeep Sharma, the spoiler for Delhi, was the man of the match
 dilli apane nunatam score 67 par simatibgaiyr captain jahir khan ke utre dilli dairedevills ko kings ilevan punjab ne 67 ran par samet diya
 Karun Nair did not like captaincy in Zaheer's absence
 ipel main dilli kaa yah nunatam score he
 Overall is the third lowest score in the IPL after 49 (RCB) and 58 (RR) runs
 keker kaa bhi nunatam score 67 he
 In Delhi's innings only three batsmen were able to touch double digits
 sandip sharma ne 4 over main 20 ran dekar 4 wicket chatkaaye
 While Akshar Patel took two wickets for 22 runs in 4 overs
 aakhir main varun aaron ne 2 over main 3 ran dekar 2 wicket nikaale
 Delhi's last five wickets fell for 37 runs at the score of 67
 shami (2 ran) ko varun aaron ne waapas bheja
 Delhi got the last blow on this score
 shahbaaj nadeem (0) ko mohit sharma ne out kiya
 Complete Team 17
 1 over main simat gai
 Before that
 rabada (11 ran) sandip sharma ko ooncha shot lagane kii koshish main lapke gaye
 Shaun Marsh took that catch
 62 ke score par dilli kaa aathvaan wicket gira
 Earlier Corey Anderson (18 runs) also could not survive
 unhen 59 ke score par varun aaron ne bold kiya
 Delhi's seventh wicket fell
 kris morris (2 ran) bhi khud ko bachaa nahin paae
 Akshar Patel bowled him
 33 ran par dilli kaa chatha wicket gira
 Half of Delhi's team returned for 30 runs, Rishabh Pant (3 runs) also kept going cheaply
 captain glen maxwell ne 30 ran par dilli ko paanchvaan jhatka diya
 In the fall of wickets, Karun Nair (11 runs) was bowled by Akshar Patel
 25 ran par dilli kaa chauthaa wicket gira
 Sanju Samson and Sam Billings opened the innings for Delhi Daredevils
 lekin pehle hi over main billings (0) kaa wicket gira
 Sandeep Sharma got him caught behind by Wriddhiman Saha
 ek ran par pehla wicket gira
 Eventually Samson hit the first four of the match off the third ball of the third over
 lekin isi over main 7 ran ke score par sanju (5 ran) out ho gaye
 Sandeep Sharma delivered the second blow
 iske baad shreyas ayyar (6 ran) ko sandip sharma ne apni hi gend par lapak liya
 The third wicket fell on a score of 22
 kings punjab ne toss jeeta, gendbaaji lipisie mohali ke aies bindra stadium main kings ilevan punjab ne toss jitkar gendbaaji kaa faisla kiya
 Kings XI Punjab and Delhi Daredevils came face to face in the 36th match of IPL-10
 achche form se ladkadhaakar chathe sthaan par pahunche punjab kaa lakshya mohali main dilli se apni haar kaa badla lenaa tha
 In the 15th match of this season, Delhi defeated Punjab by 51 runs at their home ground
 udhar, pichley chaar maichon main lagaataar haar ke baad dilli kii team apni jeet kii raah dekh rahi thi, lekin ek baar phir vah naakaam rahi
 Head to head: kings XI vs DD Both have clashed 21 times so far
 11 main kings ilevan punjab ne baaji maari

 congress par likhi gayi ek kitaab main purv pradhanmantri indira gandhi ko hindi bhashi pradeshon khaastaur par uttar pradesh main party ke chunavi aadhaar ko nuksaan pahunchane ke liye jimmedaar tehraaya gaya he
 In the fifth issue of the book 'A Sentential History of the Indian National Congress' series, it is written that Indira Gandhi tried to go to the grassroots level but with the help of her close aides made changes in the structure of the party from the top level, which she controlled Fewer people lived
 isse congress kaa mul santhnik swaroop charmara gaya jo kuch rajyon main party kii majbootee kaa aadhaar tha

" party ke niyantran ke unke prayaason ne aatanrik loktantr ko samaapt kiya jiske chalate uttar pradesh jaise pramukh rajyon main party kii shakhaon kaa patan hua
 "significantly, on the occasion of 125 years of the party's completion, this book has been prepared by a group of editors under the chairmanship of senior leader Pranab Mukherjee, in which many issues affecting the Congress have been described and analyzed
 kitaab kii prastaavna main mukherjee ne kaha he ki congress chaahati thi ki is ank kaa sampadan visheshgy karen or isamen apana yogadan den taaki jis avadhi kii samiksha kii ja rahi he us par ek uddeshyparak or vidwaanon kaa najariya saamne aaye or jaruri nahin he ki vah party kaa drushtikon ho

 pustak main ukt avadhi ke dauraan hue chah chunaavon main raajnneetik or saamaajik paridrishy kii padtaal karte hue ek lekh main sudhaa pai likhti hai, ‘‘jis vakt desh main or party main halaat (indira) gandhi ke parivartan ke drushtikon ko hasil karne ke lihaaj se paripakv the, vah vyaktigat kendrit raajnneeti main chali gayin jiske natijatan unke haathon main satta kaa kendrikaran hua

 iske mutabik, ‘‘unhone party ko nuksaan pahunchaaya, madhyavarti netritv tathaa salaah mashvira se faisla lene kii prakriya ko samaapt kar diya or apane liye vyaktigat taur par javabdeh padaadhikariyon ke saath bina loktantric dhaanche ke iskaa punarnirmaan kiya
 "it is written in the book," (indira) Gandhi inherited a well-organized party with all the competent leaders in the states across the country

 in ghatnakramon ne sanyukt taur par party ke saamaajik or kshetreey aadhaar par or iske chunavi bhavishya ko nuksaan pahunchaaya

" ’’ iske mutabik indira gandhi ke paas satta ke adhikaar ke chalate party or sarkaar main piramid kii tarah kaa nirnay lene vaala dhaancha ban gaya

 ’’ iske anusaar, ‘‘1950 or 1960 ke dashak kii tulana main 1970 ke dashak ke madhya tak party main mushkil se hi raajnneetik shakti ke swatantra aadhaar vaale rashtriya or pradesh str ke netaa the
 According to the authors, Indira Gandhi believed that her control in the party units of the states was more important than a healthy party
 hindi bhashi kshetra main party kaa aadhaar khisakane ke liye ‘apatkaal kii jyaadati’ ko jimmedaar tehraate hue pustak bayaan karti he ki congress ko nehru ke kaal main anusuchit jatiyon, anusuchit janajatiyon or alpsankhyakon se mila samarthan 1977 main apatkaal ke atyaachaar ke chalate chhin bhinn ho gaya
 According to the book, "the loss of support of Scheduled Castes and Minorities in the long haul led to loss of Congress in the Hindi speaking regions and the emergence of parties like SP, RJD and BSP
" yah congress kaa patan tha jisane in partiyon ke liye raajnneetik avasar muhaiyaa karaayaa

 India has so far had only one Dalit President, KR Narayanan
 lekin wo dakshin se aate the or uttar kii raajnneeti main unka dakhal or prabhaav na ke baraabar rahaa he

 lekin bhaajapa ko uske liye anukool maahaul banane kii zarurat he
